msg:Jiaxing, a small city next door to Shanghai, used to give people the impression of a red tour, but after the actual tour, there are ancient buildings, old streets with a sense of fireworks, and a fashionable world with a lot of background...
I booked the "Jiayuan Four Seasons Hotel" early before the May Day holiday, a hotel surrounded by scenery and green plants. When we arrived to arrange the specific room number, the front desk Xiao Han warmly received us, told us the breakfast time and the rule of one room for two people, and the meal fee for one more person is 68 yuan/person, which will be deducted from the room fee. We also arranged service staff, added an extra set of toiletries, registered the car number, and could enter and exit the hotel freely. At the same time, we were given The hand gesture is polite, and the handsome boy is quite carefulüòÄ
Entering the room, the dry and wet areas are separated, very clean, there is no cabinet with a door, but it is enough to hang clothes, the design is reasonable, and there are fruits as a gift, which is really politeüëçüëçüëç
The western restaurant on the second floor is responsible for breakfast (so-so), and the Chinese restaurant on the third floor can order food and deliver it to the room, and there are also set meals. The taste is very good. The only shortcoming is that the rice is too hard, like chewing gravel. The Yangtze River Delta, a land of fish and rice, should not lack soft and glutinous rice. In particular, Jiaxing is famous for its rice dumplings, which is enough to add a little glutinous rice to the rice, which is closely related to the city specialty of Jiaxing!
The small flaws in the restaurant do not affect the recognition of the hotel service, so it is wide‚úÖüëå

msg:The unintentional trip to Jiaxing during the Qingming Festival in 2024 brought many surprises. I didn't make any plans for this Qingming Festival. The main goal was to be spontaneous. In the end, I decided to book Jiaxing by looking at Baidu on my phone. I stayed at the Hilton Garden Inn in Jiaxing once when my baby was very young, so I planned to stay there this time. But when I checked the map, I suddenly saw the Ferris wheel, so I planned to stay closer. My usual style is to consult more before placing an order, so I called the front desk for consultation. At that time, it was Ms. Xiao Xiang who answered the phone. After patiently answering a few questions I was concerned about, she took the initiative to let me see if there was a suitable package (at that time, because I was interested in the Ferris wheel, there was a special package with tickets), which made me completely abandon the Hilton Garden Inn (sorry, human nature is to explore). After studying the package, I finally booked a two-night package. Xiao Xiang also helped me to note the specific matters such as the view room and the sofa, which was also confirmed when I checked in later. Thank you! Next, let's talk about the facilities. They are simple but warm. This is the feeling when you see them for the first time. Jiayuan Four Seasons does not have the kind of luxurious first vision that blinds the eyes, but the software is still up to date, including the souvenirs for the first day of check-in, and the car license plate is registered in the system. The elevator goes directly to the 18th floor. You must swipe your card to get to the floor you live in, which greatly increases the safety factor. After entering the room, it was a little hot and the ventilation was slightly poor, but it was not summer yet, so it was estimated that the air conditioning system had not been fully turned on. We wanted a twin room, and the two 1.35-meter beds were more comfortable. The large floor-to-ceiling windows could directly see the Ferris wheel and the big square outside the window. The auntie was also very considerate to send towels and toothbrushes, help clean, and send fruits every day... The feeling of home came. When checking out this morning, the handsome guy thoughtfully helped to check out, which was fast and complete, and called back in time after arriving home. Sorry, I can't remember what he called me. However, there will definitely be a chance to see you again. After all, a pleasant stay is the beginning of the next goodbye!

Swimming pool: 1.2--1.5 meters, full of children taking swimming lessons (probably rented out). This is the first time I encountered this kind of hotel swimming pool.
